@jwt_required()\n        def decorated(*args, **kwargs):\n            user_id = get_jwt_identity()\n            user = User.query.get(user_id)\n            if user and user.role in roles:\n                return fn(*args, **kwargs)\n            else:\n                return jsonify({'msg': 'Unauthorized'}), 403\n        decorated.__name__ = fn.__name__\n        return decorated\n    return                         "import uuid\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Optional\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# --------------------------\n# Data Models\n# --------------------------\n\nclass User:\n    def __init__(self, username: str, password: str, is_provider: bool = False, is_admin: bool = False):\n        self.user_id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        self.username = username\n        self.password = password  # NOTE: In production, never store plain passwords!\n        self.is_provider = is_provider\n        self.is_admin = is_admin\n\n    def __repr__(self):\n        return f\"<User {self.username} {'[Provider]' if self.is_provider else ''} {'[Admin]' if self.is_admin else ''}>\"\n\n\nclass ProviderProfile:\n    def __init__(self, user: User, skills: List[str], bio: str):\n        self.provider_id = user.user_id\n        self.skills = skills\n        self.bio = bio\n        self.rating = 0.0\n        self.num_ratings = 0\n\n    def update_rating(self, new_rating: float):\n        total = self.rating * self.num_ratings + new_rating\n        self.num_ratings += 1\n        self.rating = total / self.num_ratings\n\n    def __repr__(self):\n        return f\"<ProviderProfile {self.provider_id} | Skills: {self.skills} | Rating: {self.rating:.2f}>\"\n\n\nclass ServiceRequest:\n    def __init__(self, customer: User, service_type: str, description: str):\n        self.request_id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        self.customer_id = customer.user_id\n        self.provider_id: Optional[str] = None\n        self.service_type = service_type\n        self.description = description\n        self.status = \"Pending\"  # Pending, Accepted, In Progress, Completed, Cancelled\n        self.created_at = datetime.now()\n        self.updated_at = datetime.now()\n        self.invoice: Optional['Invoice'] = None\n\n    def assign_provider(self, provider_id: str):\n        self.provider_id = provider_id\n        self.status = \"Accepted\"\n        self.updated_at = datetime.now()\n\n    def update_status(self, new_status: str):\n        self.status = new_status\n        self.updated_at = datetime.now()\n\n    def __repr__(self):\n        return f\"<ServiceRequest {self.request_id} | {self.service_type} | Status: {self.status}>\"\n\n\nclass Invoice:\n    COMMISSION_RATE = 0.05  # 5%\n\n    def __init__(self, service_request: ServiceRequest, amount: float):\n        self.invoice_id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        self.request_id = service_request.request_id\n        self.amount = amount\n        self.commission = round(amount * self.COMMISSION_RATE, 2)\n        self.total = round(amount + self.commission, 2)\n        self.created_at = datetime.now()\n        self.paid = False\n\n    def mark_paid(self):\n        self.paid = True\n\n    def __repr__(self):\n        return f\"<Invoice {self.invoice_id} | Amount: {self.amount} | Commission: {self.commission} | Paid: {self.paid}>\"\n\n\n# --------------------------\n# Platform Core\n# --------------------------\n\nclass Platform:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.users: Dict[str, User] = {}\n        self.provider_profiles: Dict[str, ProviderProfile] = {}\n        self.requests: Dict[str, ServiceRequest] = {}\n        self.invoices: Dict[str, Invoice] = {}\n        self.current_user: Optional[User] = None\n\n    # --- Authentication ---\n    def register(self, username: str, password: str, is_provider: bool = False, is_admin: bool = False):\n        if username in [u.username for u in self.users.values()]:\n            print(\"Username already exists.\")\n            return None\n        user = User(username, password, is_provider, is_admin)\n        self.users[user.user_id] = user\n        print(f\"User registered: {user}\")\n        return user\n\n    def login(self, username: str, password: str) -> bool:\n        for user in self.users.values():\n            if user.username == username and user.password == password:\n                self.current_user = user\n                print(f\"Logged in as {user.username}\")\n                return True\n        print(\"Invalid credentials.\")\n        return False\n\n    def logout(self):\n        if self.current_user:\n            print(f\"User {self.current_user.username} logged out.\")\n            self.current_user = None\n\n    # --- Provider Profile ---\n    def create_provider_profile(self, skills: List[str], bio: str):\n        if not self.current_user or not self.current_user.is_provider:\n            print(\"Only providers can create profiles.\")\n            return\n        profile = ProviderProfile(self.current_user, skills, bio)\n        self.provider_profiles[self.current_user.user_id] = profile\n        print(f\"Provider profile created: {profile}\")\n\n    def view_providers(self):\n        for profile in self.provider_profiles.values():\n            print(profile)\n\n    # --- Service Requests ---\n    def create_service_request(self, service_type: str, description: str):\n        if not self.current_user or self.current_user.is_provider:\n            print(\"Only customers can create service requests.\")\n            return\n        req = ServiceRequest(self.current_user, service_type, description)\n        self.requests[req.request_id] = req\n        print(f\"Service request created: {req}\")\n\n    def view_my_requests(self):\n        if not self.current_user:\n            print(\"Login required.\")\n            return\n        for req in self.requests.values():\n            if req.customer_id == self.current_user.user_id or req.provider_id == self.current_user.user_id:\n                print(req)\n\n    def assign_provider_to_request(self, request_id: str, provider_id: str):\n        if request_id in self.requests and provider_id in self.provider_profiles:\n            req = self.requests[request_id]\n            if req.status != \"Pending\":\n                print(\"Request already assigned or not available.\")\n                return\n            req.assign_provider(provider_id)\n            print(f\"Provider assigned: {req}\")\n        else:\n            print(\"Invalid request or provider.\")\n\n    def update_request_status(self, request_id: str, new_status: str):\n        if request_id in self.requests:\n            req = self.requests[request_id]\n            if self.current_user.user_id not in [req.provider_id, req.customer_id] and not self.current_user.is_admin:\n                print(\"Not authorized.\")\n                return\n            req.update_status(new_status)\n            print(f\"Status updated: {req}\")\n        else:\n            print(\"Request not found.\")\n\n    # --- Invoicing ---\n    def generate_invoice(self, request_id: str, amount: float):\n        if request_id in self.requests:\n            req = self.requests[request_id]\n            if not req.provider_id:\n                print(\"No provider assigned.\")\n                return\n            invoice = Invoice(req, amount)\n            self.invoices[invoice.invoice_id] = invoice\n            req.invoice = invoice\n            print(f\"Invoice generated: {invoice}\")\n        else:\n            print(\"Request not found.\")\n\n    def pay_invoice(self, invoice_id: str):\n        if invoice_id in self.invoices:\n            invoice = self.invoices[invoice_id]\n            invoice.mark_paid()\n            print(f\"Invoice paid: {invoice}\")\n        else:\n            print(\"Invoice not found.\")\n\n    # --- Admin Panel ---\n    def admin_list_users(self):\n        if not self.current_user or not self.current_user.is_admin:\n            print(\"Admin access required.\")\n            return\n        for user in self.users.values():\n            print(user)\n\n    def admin_list_requests(self):\n        if not self.current_user or not self.current_user.is_admin:\n            print(\"Admin access required.\")\n            return\n        for req in self.requests.values():\n            print(req)\n\n    def admin_list_invoices(self):\n        if not self.current_user or not self.current_user.is_admin:\n            print(\"Admin access required.\")\n            return\n        for inv in self.invoices.values():\n            print(inv)\n\n    def admin_remove_user(self, user_id: str):\n        if not self.current_user or not self.current_user.is_admin:\n            print(\"Admin access required.\")\n            return\n        if user_id in self.users:\n            del self.users[user_id]\n            self.provider_profiles.pop(user_id, None)\n            print(f\"User {user_id} removed.\")\n        else:\n            print(\"User not found.\")\n\n# --------------------------\n# Simple CLI for Demo\n# --------------------------\n\ndef demo():\n    platform = Platform()\n\n    # Register users\n    admin = platform.register(\"admin\", \"adminpass\", is_admin=True)\n    cust = platform.register(\"alice\", \"alicepass\")\n    prov = platform.register(\"bob\", \"bobpass\", is_provider=True)\n\n    # Login as provider and create profile\n    platform.login(\"bob\", \"bobpass\")\n    platform.create_provider_profile([\"plumbing\", \"electrical\"], \"Experienced handyman.\")\n    platform.logout()\n\n    # Login as customer and create service request\n    platform.login(\"alice\", \"alicepass\")\n    platform.create_service_request(\"plumbing\", \"Leaky faucet in kitchen.\")\n    platform.logout()\n\n    # Admin assigns provider to request\n    platform.login(\"admin\", \"adminpass\")\n    req_id = next(iter(platform.requests))\n    provider_id = prov.user_id\n    platform.assign_provider_to_request(req_id, provider_id)\n    platform.logout()\n\n    # Provider generates invoice\n    platform.login(\"bob\", \"bobpass\")\n    platform.generate_invoice(req_id, 100.0)  # $100 service\n    invoice_id = next(iter(platform.invoices))\n    platform.logout()\n\n    # Customer pays invoice\n    platform.login(\"alice\", \"alicepass\")\n    platform.pay_invoice(invoice_id)\n    platform.logout()\n\n    # Admin views all\n    platform.login(\"admin\", \"adminpass\")\n    print(\"\\n--- USERS ---\")\n    platform.admin_list_users()\n    print(\"\\n--- REQUESTS ---\")\n    platform.admin_list_requests()\n    print(\"\\n--- INVOICES ---\")\n    platform.admin_list_invoices()\n    platform.logout()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    demo()"

Provider sees available requests\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/requests/available\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        available = resp.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(r[\"id\"] == req_id for r in available))\n\n    def test_accept_request_and_status_updates(self):\n        # Customer creates a request\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/requests/\", headers=headers, data={\n            \"description\": \"Fix my sink\"\n        })\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        # Provider accepts\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Request accepted\", resp.text)\n        # Provider updates status to in_progress\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers=headers, data={\n            \"status\": \"in_progress\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Status updated to in_progress\", resp.text)\n        # Provider updates status to completed\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers=headers, data={\n            \"status\": \"completed\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Status updated to completed\", resp.text)\n        # Invoice should be created\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = resp.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(inv[\"service_request_id\"] == req_id for inv in invoices))\n\n    def test_invoice_payment(self):\n        # Full flow: customer creates request, provider accepts, completes, customer pays invoice\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/requests/\", headers=headers, data={\n            \"description\": \"Install ceiling fan\"\n        })\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        # Provider accepts and completes\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=headers)\n        self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers=headers, data={\"status\": \"completed\"})\n        # Customer gets invoice\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers=headers)\n        invoices = resp.json()\n        self.assertTrue(len(invoices) > 0)\n        invoice_id = invoices[0][\"id\"]\n        self.assertFalse(invoices[0][\"paid\"])\n        # Customer pays invoice\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/invoices/{invoice_id}/pay\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Invoice marked as paid\", resp.text)\n        # Verify paid\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertTrue(resp.json()[0][\"paid\"])\n\n    def test_only_provider_can_accept(self):\n        # Customer creates request\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/requests/\", headers=headers, data={\n            \"description\": \"Paint my house\"\n        })\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        # Customer tries to accept (should fail)\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        self.assertIn(\"Not a provider\", resp.text)\n\n    def test_status_update_authorization(self):\n        # Customer creates request, provider accepts\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/requests/\", headers=headers, data={\n            \"description\": \"Clean my yard\"\n        })\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=headers)\n        # Another provider tries to update status (should fail)\n        # Register second provider\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/register/\", data={\n            \"username\": \"provider2\",\n            \"password\": \"prov2pass\",\n            \"role\": \"provider\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        token2 = self._login(\"provider2\", \"prov2pass\")\n        headers2 = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {token2}\"}\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers=headers2, data={\n            \"status\": \"in_progress\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        self.assertIn(\"Not authorized\", resp.text)\n\n    def test_admin_panel_access(self):\n        # Admin lists users\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/admin/users\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        users = resp.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(u[\"username\"] == self.customer_username for u in users))\n        # Non-admin tries to access\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/admin/users\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        self.assertIn(\"Not enough permissions\", resp.text)\n\n    def test_admin_deactivate_user(self):\n        # Admin deactivates provider\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"}\n        # Get provider user id\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/admin/users\", headers=headers)\n        users = resp.json()\n        provider_user = next(u for u in users if u[\"username\"] == self.provider_username)\n        provider_id = provider_user[\"id\"]\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/admin/users/{provider_id}/deactivate\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"User deactivated\", resp.text)\n        # Provider cannot login anymore\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/token\", data={\n            \"username\": self.provider_username,\n            \"password\": self.provider_password\n        })\n        # Still can login, but should be forbidden for actions\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        token = resp.json()[\"access_token\"]\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/providers/me\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"Inactive user\", resp.text)\n\n    def test_edge_case_cancelled_request(self):\n        # Customer creates request, provider accepts, customer cancels\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/requests/\", headers=headers, data={\n            \"description\": \"Mow the lawn\"\n        })\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=headers)\n        # Customer cancels\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers=headers, data={\n            \"status\": \"cancelled\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Status updated to cancelled\", resp.text)\n        # Provider cannot update status anymore\n        headers = {\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers=headers, data={\n            \"status\": \"in_progress\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        self.assertIn(\"Not authorized\", resp.text)\n\n    def test_invoice_commission_calculation(self):\n        #                         "import unittest\nfrom fastapi.testclient import TestClient\nfrom sqlalchemy import create_engine\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker\nimport sys\nimport os\n\n# Import the app and models from the provided code\n# Assume the code is in a file named 'on_demand_services.py'\n# If running in the same file, you can do: from __main__ import app, Base, SessionLocal, UserRole, ServiceStatus\n\n# For this test suite, we assume the code is available in the current namespace\n# If not, replace 'from __main__' with 'from on_demand_services'\n\nfrom __main__ import (\n    app,\n    Base,\n    SessionLocal,\n    UserRole,\n    ServiceStatus,\n    User,\n    ProviderProfile,\n    ServiceRequest,\n    Invoice,\n    get_password_hash,\n    SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URL,\n)\n\n# Use a separate in-memory SQLite DB for testing\nTEST_SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URL = \"sqlite:///./test_on_demand_services.db\"\nengine = create_engine(TEST_SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URL, connect_args={\"check_same_thread\": False})\nTestingSessionLocal = sessionmaker(autocommit=False, autoflush=False, bind=engine)\n\n# Patch the app's SessionLocal to use the test DB\ndef override_get_db():\n    db = TestingSessionLocal()\n    try:\n        yield db\n    finally:\n        db.close()\n\napp.dependency_overrides[SessionLocal] = TestingSessionLocal\napp.dependency_overrides['get_db'] = override_get_db\n\nclient = TestClient(app)\n\ndef setUpModule():\n    # Ensure a clean DB for each test class\n        Base.metadata.drop_all(bind=engine)\n        Base.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)\n\n        # Register users: customer, provider, admin\n        cls.customer_username = \"customer1\"\n        cls.provider_username = \"provider1\"\n        cls.admin_username = \"admin1\"\n        cls.password = \"password123\"\n\n        # Register customer\n        response = client.post(\"/register/\", data={\n            \"username\": cls.customer_username,\n            \"password\": cls.password,\n            \"role\": UserRole.customer.value\n        })\n        assert response.status_code == 200\n\n        # Register provider\n        response = client.post(\"/register/\", data={\n            \"username\": cls.provider_username,\n            \"password\": cls.password,\n            \"role\": UserRole.provider.value\n        })\n        assert response.status_code == 200\n\n        # Register admin\n        response = client.post(\"/register/\", data={\n            \"username\": cls.admin_username,\n            \"password\": cls.password,\n            \"role\": UserRole.admin.value\n        })\n        assert response.status_code == 200\n\n        # Get tokens\n        cls.customer_token = cls.login(cls.customer_username, cls.password)\n        cls.provider_token = cls.login(cls.provider_username, cls.password)\n        cls.admin_token = cls.login(cls.admin_username, cls.password)\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def login(username, password):\n        response = client.post(\"/token\", data={\n            \"username\": username,\n            \"password\": password\n        })\n        assert response.status_code == 200\n        return response.json()[\"access_token\"]\n\n    def test_register_duplicate_username(self):\n        # Try to register with an existing username\n        response = client.post(\"/register/\", data={\n            \"username\": self.customer_username,\n            \"password\": \"newpassword\",\n            \"role\": UserRole.customer.value\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"Username already registered\", response.text)\n\n    def test_login_wrong_password(self):\n        response = client.post(\"/token\", data={\n            \"username\": self.customer_username,\n            \"password\": \"wrongpassword\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"Incorrect username or password\", response.text)\n\n    def test_provider_profile_creation_and_update(self):\n        # Provider profile should exist after registration\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/providers/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        profile = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"full_name\"], \"\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"bio\"], \"\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"skills\"], \"\")\n\n        # Update profile\n        response = client.put(\n            \"/providers/me\",\n            data={\n                \"full_name\": \"Jane Provider\",\n                \"bio\": \"Expert in cleaning\",\n                \"skills\": \"cleaning, organizing\"\n            },\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Profile updated\", response.text)\n\n        # Get profile again\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/providers/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        profile = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"full_name\"], \"Jane Provider\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"bio\"], \"Expert in cleaning\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"skills\"], \"cleaning, organizing\")\n\n    def test_list_providers(self):\n        response = client.get(\"/providers/\")\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        providers = response.json()\n        self.assertIsInstance(providers, list)\n        self.assertTrue(any(p[\"username\"] == self.provider_username for p in providers))\n\n    def test_create_service_request_and_status_flow(self):\n        # Customer creates a request\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/requests/\",\n            data={\"description\": \"Need house cleaning\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        req = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(req[\"status\"], ServiceStatus.requested)\n        request_id = req[\"id\"]\n\n        # Provider lists available requests\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/requests/available\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        available = response.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(r[\"id\"] == request_id for r in available))\n\n        # Provider accepts the request\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{request_id}/accept\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Request accepted\", response.text)\n\n        # Provider updates status to in_progress\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{request_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": ServiceStatus.in_progress.value},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(ServiceStatus.in_progress, response.text)\n\n        # Provider cannot update status for a request they don't own\n        # Create a second provider\n        response = client.post(\"/register/\", data={\n            \"username\": \"provider2\",\n            \"password\": self.password,\n            \"role\": UserRole.provider.value\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        provider2_token = self.login(\"provider2\", self.password)\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{request_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": ServiceStatus.completed.value},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {provider2_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 403)\n\n        # Customer updates status to completed\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{request_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": ServiceStatus.completed.value},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(ServiceStatus.completed, response.text)\n\n        # Invoice should be created\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/invoices/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = response.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(inv[\"service_request_id\"] == request_id for inv in invoices))\n        invoice = next(inv for inv in invoices if inv[\"service_request_id\"] == request_id)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(invoice[\"amount\"], 100.0)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(invoice[\"commission\"], 5.0)\n        self.assertFalse(invoice[\"paid\"])\n\n        # Customer pays invoice\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/invoices/{invoice['id']}/pay\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Invoice marked as paid\", response.text)\n\n        # Invoice should now be marked as paid\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/invoices/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        invoices = response.json()\n        invoice = next(inv for inv in invoices if inv[\"id\"] == invoice[\"id\"])\n        self.assertTrue(invoice[\"paid\"])\n\n    def test_my_requests(self):\n        # Customer creates two requests\n        ids = []\n        for i in range(2):\n            response = client.post(\n                \"/requests/\",\n                data={\"description\": f\"Service {i}\"},\n                headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n            )\n            self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n            ids.append(response.json()[\"id\"])\n        # Customer lists their requests\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/requests/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        reqs = response.json()\n        self.assertTrue(all(r[\"id\"] in ids for r in reqs))\n\n    def test_admin_panel(self):\n        # Admin lists users\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/admin/users\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        users = response.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(u[\"username\"] == self.customer_username for u in users))\n        self.assertTrue(any(u[\"username\"] == self.provider_username for u in users))\n        self.assertTrue(any(u[\"username\"] == self.admin_username for u in users))\n\n        # Admin lists requests\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/admin/requests\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        requests = response.json()\n        self.assertIsInstance(requests, list)\n\n        # Admin lists invoices\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/admin/invoices\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = response.json()\n        self.assertIsInstance(invoices, list)\n\n        # Admin deactivates a user\n        # First, get a user ID\n        user_id = next(u[\"id\"] for u in users if u[\"username\"] == self.customer_username)\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/admin/users/{user_id}/deactivate\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"User deactivated\", response.text)\n\n        # The deactivated user should not be able to login anymore\n        response = client.post(\"/token\", data={\n            \"username\": self.customer_username,\n            \"password\": self.password\n        })\n        # They can get a token, but API should reject as inactive\n        token = response.json().get(\"access_token\")\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/requests/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"Inactive user\", response.text)\n\n    def test_permissions(self):\n        # Provider tries to create a service request (should fail)\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/requests/\",\n            data={\"description\": \"Provider trying to create request\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 403)\n\n        # Customer tries to access provider-only endpoint\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/providers/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 403)\n\n        # Customer tries to access admin-only endpoint\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/admin/users\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 403)\n\n    def test_root_endpoint(self):\n        response = client.get(\"/\")\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"On-Demand Service Platform API is running.\", response.text)\n\n    def test_edge_case_invalid_status_update(self):\n        # Customer creates a request\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/requests/\",\n            data={\"description\": \"Edge case status\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        request_id = response.json()[\"id\"]\n\n        # Try to update status with invalid status\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{request_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"not_a_status\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 422)  # Unprocessable Entity\n\n    def test_edge_case_nonexistent_request_accept(self):\n        # Provider tries to accept a non-existent request\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/requests/9999/accept\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"Request not available\", response.text)\n\n    def test_edge_case_nonexistent_invoice_pay(self):\n        # Customer tries to pay a non-existent invoice\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/invoices/9999/pay\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 404)\n        self.assertIn(\"Invoice not found\", response.text)\n\n    def test_edge_case_nonexistent_user_deactivate(self):\n        # Admin tries to deactivate a non-existent user\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/admin/users/9999/deactivate\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 404)\n        self.assertIn(\"User not found\", response.text)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    unittest.main()",
                        "import unittest\nfrom fastapi.testclient import TestClient\nfrom sqlalchemy import create_engine\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker\nimport sys\nimport os\n\n# Import the FastAPI app and models from the original code.\n# For this test script, we assume the code above is in a file named \"on_demand_services.py\"\n# If you are running in the same script, you can just import them directly.\n# For this answer, we'll use exec to load the code into the global namespace.\n\n# Load the code to test\nCODE_TO_TEST = \"\"\"\n<PASTE THE ORIGINAL CODE HERE>\n\"\"\"\n\n# For this answer, we assume the code is already loaded in the global namespace.\n# If running separately, replace this with:\n# from on_demand_services import app, Base, engine, SessionLocal, UserRole, ServiceStatus\n\n# Setup the test client\nfrom fastapi import FastAPI\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\n\napp = globals()[\"app\"]\nBase = globals()[\"Base\"]\nengine = globals()[\"engine\"]\nSessionLocal = globals()[\"SessionLocal\"]\nUserRole = globals()[\"UserRole\"]\nServiceStatus = globals()[\"ServiceStatus\"]\n\nclient = TestClient(app)\n\ndef reset_database():\n    # Drop and recreate all tables for isolation\n    Base.metadata.drop_all(bind=engine)\n    Base.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)\n\nclass OnDemandServiceTests(unittest.TestCase):\n    @classmethod\n    def setUpClass(cls):\n        reset_database()\n\n    def setUp(self):\n        reset_database()\n        self.customer_token = self._register_and_login(\"customer1\", \"pass\", UserRole.customer)\n        self.provider_token = self._register_and_login(\"provider1\", \"pass\", UserRole.provider)\n        self.admin_token = self._register_and_login(\"admin1\", \"pass\", UserRole.admin)\n\n    def _register_and_login(self, username, password, role):\n        # Register\n        resp = client.post(\"/register/\", data={\n            \"username\": username,\n            \"password\": password,\n            \"role\": role.value\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Login\n        resp = client.post(\"/token\", data={\n            \"username\": username,\n            \"password\": password\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        return resp.json()[\"access_token\"]\n\n    def test_register_duplicate_username(self):\n        resp = client.post(\"/register/\", data={\n            \"username\": \"customer1\",\n            \"password\": \"pass\",\n            \"role\": UserRole.customer.value\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"Username already registered\", resp.text)\n\n    def test_login_invalid_credentials(self):\n        resp = client.post(\"/token\", data={\n            \"username\": \"customer1\",\n            \"password\": \"wrongpass\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"Incorrect username or password\", resp.text)\n\n    def test_provider_profile_creation_and_update(self):\n        # Get provider profile\n        resp = client.get(\"/providers/me\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        profile = resp.json()\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"full_name\"], \"\")\n        # Update provider profile\n        resp = client.put(\"/providers/me\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"},\n                          data={\"full_name\": \"John Doe\", \"bio\": \"Expert\", \"skills\": \"Plumbing\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Get updated profile\n        resp = client.get(\"/providers/me\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        profile = resp.json()\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"full_name\"], \"John Doe\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"bio\"], \"Expert\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"skills\"], \"Plumbing\")\n\n    def test_list_providers(self):\n        resp = client.get(\"/providers/\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        providers = resp.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(providers), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(providers[0][\"username\"], \"provider1\")\n\n    def test_create_service_request_and_flow(self):\n        # Customer creates request\n        resp = client.post(\"/requests/\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"},\n                           data={\"description\": \"Fix my sink\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        # Provider lists available requests\n        resp = client.get(\"/requests/available\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        available = resp.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(r[\"id\"] == req_id for r in available))\n        # Provider accepts request\n        resp = client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Provider updates status to in_progress\n        resp = client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"},\n                           data={\"status\": ServiceStatus.in_progress.value})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Provider updates status to completed (triggers invoice)\n        resp = client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"},\n                           data={\"status\": ServiceStatus.completed.value})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Customer lists invoices\n        resp = client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = resp.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(invoices), 1)\n        invoice = invoices[0]\n        self.assertEqual(invoice[\"amount\"], 100.0)\n        self.assertEqual(invoice[\"commission\"], 5.0)\n        self.assertFalse(invoice[\"paid\"])\n        # Customer pays invoice\n        resp = client.post(f\"/invoices/{invoice['id']}/pay\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Invoice marked as paid\n        resp = client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = resp.json()\n        self.assertTrue(invoices[0][\"paid\"])\n\n    def test_request_status_update_authorization(self):\n        # Customer creates request\n        resp = client.post(\"/requests/\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"},\n                           data={\"description\": \"Fix my sink\"})\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        # Provider cannot update status before accepting\n        resp = client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"},\n                           data={\"status\": ServiceStatus.in_progress.value})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        # Accept request\n        client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"})\n        # Other provider cannot update status\n        other_provider_token = self._register_and_login(\"provider2\", \"pass\", UserRole.provider)\n        resp = client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {other_provider_token}\"},\n                           data={\"status\": ServiceStatus.in_progress.value})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        # Customer cannot update status of other's request\n        other_customer_token = self._register_and_login(\"customer2\", \"pass\", UserRole.customer)\n        resp = client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {other_customer_token}\"},\n                           data={\"status\": ServiceStatus.in_progress.value})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        # Customer can update status\n        resp = client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"},\n                           data={\"status\": ServiceStatus.cancelled.value})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n\n    def test_admin_panel_access_and_user_deactivation(self):\n        # Non-admin cannot access admin endpoints\n        resp = client.get(\"/admin/users\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        # Admin can list users\n        resp = client.get(\"/admin/users\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        users = resp.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(users), 3)\n        # Admin deactivates a user\n        user_id = users[0][\"id\"]\n        resp = client.post(f\"/admin/users/{user_id}/deactivate\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Deactivated user cannot login\n        username = users[0][\"username\"]\n        resp = client.post(\"/token\", data={\"username\": username, \"password\": \"pass\"})\n        # If the user is not active, login still works (token issued), but other endpoints will fail\n        # Let's check profile endpoint for provider\n        if users[0][\"role\"] == UserRole.provider.value:\n            token = resp.json()[\"access_token\"]\n            resp2 = client.get(\"/providers/me\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {token}\"})\n            self.assertEqual(resp2.status_code, 400)\n            self.assertIn(\"Inactive user\", resp2.text)\n\n    def test_edge_cases(self):\n        # Accepting non-existent request\n        resp = client.post(\"/requests/999/accept\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        # Updating status for non-existent request\n        resp = client.post(\"/requests/999/status\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"},\n                           data={\"status\": ServiceStatus.in_progress.value})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n        # Paying non-existent invoice\n        resp = client.post(\"/invoices/999/pay\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n        # Admin deactivates non-existent user\n        resp = client.post(\"/admin/users/999/deactivate\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n\n    def test_root_endpoint(self):\n        resp = client.get(\"/\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"On-Demand Service Platform API is running.\", resp.text)\n\n    def test_invoice_access_for_provider(self):\n        # Customer creates request\n        resp = client.post(\"/requests/\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"},\n                           data={\"description\": \"Fix my sink\"})\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        # Duplicate username\n        response = self.register_user(\"cust1\", \"pass789\", \"customer\")\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 400)\n\n        # Login success\n        login = self.login_user(\"cust1\", \"pass123\")\n        self.assertEqual(login.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"access_token\", login.json())\n\n        # Login failure\n        login = self.login_user(\"cust1\", \"wrongpass\")\n        self.assertEqual(login.status_code, 400)\n\n        # Login non-existent user\n        login = self.login_user(\"nouser\", \"nopass\")\n        self.assertEqual(login.status_code, 400)\n\n    def test_provider_profile_crud(self):\n        self.register_user(\"prov1\", \"pass456\", \"provider\")\n        headers = self.get_auth_header(\"prov1\", \"pass456\")\n\n        # Get empty profile\n        response = self.client.get(\"/providers/me\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        profile = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"full_name\"], \"\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"bio\"], \"\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"skills\"], \"\")\n\n        # Update profile\n        response = self.client.put(\n            \"/providers/me\",\n            data={\"full_name\": \"John Doe\", \"bio\": \"Expert\", \"skills\": \"Plumbing,Electrical\"},\n            headers=headers\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"msg\", response.json())\n\n        # Get updated profile\n        response = self.client.get(\"/providers/me\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        profile = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"full_name\"], \"John Doe\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"bio\"], \"Expert\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"skills\"], \"Plumbing,Electrical\")\n\n        # List all providers\n        response = self.client.get(\"/providers/\")\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        providers = response.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(p[\"username\"] == \"prov1\" for p in providers))\n\n        # Customer cannot access provider profile\n        self.register_user(\"cust1\", \"pass123\", \"customer\")\n        cust_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"cust1\", \"pass123\")\n        response = self.client.get(\"/providers/me\", headers=cust_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 403)\n\n    def test_service_request_flow(self):\n        # Register users\n        self.register_user(\"cust1\", \"pass123\", \"customer\")\n        self.register_user(\"prov1\", \"pass456\", \"provider\")\n        cust_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"cust1\", \"pass123\")\n        prov_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"prov1\", \"pass456\")\n\n        # Customer creates request\n        response = self.client.post(\n            \"/requests/\",\n            data={\"description\": \"Fix my sink\"},\n            headers=cust_headers\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        req_id = response.json()[\"id\"]\n\n        # Provider lists available requests\n        response = self.client.get(\"/requests/available\", headers=prov_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        available = response.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(r[\"id\"] == req_id for r in available))\n\n        # Provider accepts request\n        response = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=prov_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"msg\", response.json())\n\n        # Provider cannot accept again\n        response = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=prov_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 400)\n\n        # Provider updates status to in_progress\n        response = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"in_progress\"},\n            headers=prov_headers\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n\n        # Customer updates status to completed (simulate completion)\n        response = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"},\n            headers=cust_headers\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n\n        # Invoice should be created\n        response = self.client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers=cust_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = response.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(inv[\"service_request_id\"] == req_id for inv in invoices))\n        invoice_id = invoices[0][\"id\"]\n\n        # Customer pays invoice\n        response = self.client.post(f\"/invoices/{invoice_id}/pay\", headers=cust_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"msg\", response.json())\n\n        # Invoice marked as paid\n        response = self.client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers=cust_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = response.json()\n        self.assertTrue(invoices[0][\"paid\"])\n\n        # Provider can see invoice\n        response = self.client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers=prov_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        provider_invoices = response.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(inv[\"service_request_id\"] == req_id for inv in provider_invoices))\n\n        # Edge: Provider cannot pay invoice\n        response = self.client.post(f\"/invoices/{invoice_id}/pay\", headers=prov_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 403)\n\n    def test_live_status_update_edge_cases(self):\n        self.register_user(\"cust1\", \"pass123\", \"customer\")\n        self.register_user(\"prov1\", \"pass456\", \"provider\")\n        cust_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"cust1\", \"pass123\")\n        prov_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"prov1\", \"pass456\")\n\n        # Customer creates request\n        response = self.client.post(\n            \"/requests/\",\n            data={\"description\": \"Test status\"},\n            headers=cust_headers\n        )\n        req_id = response.json()[\"id\"]\n\n        # Provider accepts request\n        self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=prov_headers)\n\n        # Unauthorized user tries to update status\n        self.register_user(\"other\", \"pass789\", \"customer\")\n        other_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"other\", \"pass789\")\n        response = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"cancelled\"},\n            headers=other_headers\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 403)\n\n        # Provider updates status to completed, invoice created\n        response = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"},\n            headers=prov_headers\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n\n        # Try updating status for non-existent request\n        response = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/9999/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"},\n            headers=prov_headers\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 404)\n\n    def test_admin_panel_access_and_management(self):\n        # Non-admin cannot access admin endpoints\n        response = self.client.get(\"/admin/users\", headers=cust_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 403)\n\n        # Admin deactivates a user\n        user_id = next(u[\"id\"] for u in users if u[\"username\"] == \"cust1\")\n        response = self.client.post(f\"/admin/users/{user_id}/deactivate\", headers=admin_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"msg\", response.json())\n\n        # Deactivated user cannot login\n        login = self.login_user(\"cust1\", \"pass123\")\n        self.assertEqual(login.status_code, 200)\n        token = login.json()[\"access_token\"]\n        # Try to access as deactivated user\n        response = self.client.get(\"/requests/me\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 400)  # inactive user\n\n    def test_edge_cases_and_invalid_inputs(self):\n        # Register users\n        self.register_user(\"cust1\", \"pass123\", \"customer\")\n        self.register_user(\"prov1\", \"pass456\", \"provider\")\n        cust_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"cust1\", \"pass123\")\n        prov_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"prov1\", \"pass456\")\n\n        # Non-existent user\n        resp = self.login_user(\"notfound\", \"password123\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n\n    def test_provider_profile_flow(self):\n        self.register_user(\"bob\", \"password123\", \"provider\")\n        headers = self.get_auth_header(\"bob\", \"password123\")\n        # Get my profile (should be empty)\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/providers/me\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        profile = resp.json()\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"full_name\"], \"\")\n        # Update profile\n        resp = self.client.put(\n            \"/providers/me\",\n            headers=headers,\n            data={\"full_name\": \"Bob Builder\", \"bio\": \"Expert\", \"skills\": \"Plumbing\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.json()[\"msg\"], \"Profile updated\")\n        # Get updated profile\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/providers/me\", headers=headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        profile = resp.json()\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"full_name\"], \"Bob Builder\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"bio\"], \"Expert\")\n        self.assertEqual(profile[\"skills\"], \"Plumbing\")\n        # List all providers\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/providers/\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        providers = resp.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(p[\"username\"] == \"bob\" for p in providers))\n\n    def test_service_request_flow_and_edge_cases(self):\n        # Register users\n        self.register_user(\"alice\", \"password123\", \"customer\")\n        self.register_user(\"bob\", \"password123\", \"provider\")\n        alice_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"alice\", \"password123\")\n        bob_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"bob\", \"password123\")\n        # Customer creates request\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/requests/\", headers=alice_headers, data={\"description\": \"Fix sink\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        # Provider lists available requests\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/requests/available\", headers=bob_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertTrue(any(r[\"id\"] == req_id for r in resp.json()))\n        # Provider accepts request\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=bob_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.json()[\"msg\"], \"Request accepted\")\n        # Provider tries to accept again (should fail)\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=bob_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        # Customer tries to accept (should fail)\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=alice_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        # Provider updates status to in_progress\n        resp = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            headers=bob_headers,\n            data={\"status\": \"in_progress\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Customer tries to update status of another user's request (should fail)\n        self.register_user(\"eve\", \"password123\", \"customer\")\n        eve_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"eve\", \"password123\")\n        resp = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            headers=eve_headers,\n            data={\"status\": \"cancelled\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        # Provider tries to update status of unrelated request (should fail)\n        self.register_user(\"carol\", \"password123\", \"provider\")\n        carol_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"carol\", \"password123\")\n        resp = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            headers=carol_headers,\n            data={\"status\": \"cancelled\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        # Customer updates status to completed\n        resp = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            headers=alice_headers,\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Get my requests (customer)\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/requests/me\", headers=alice_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertTrue(any(r[\"id\"] == req_id for r in resp.json()))\n        # Get my requests (provider)\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/requests/me\", headers=bob_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertTrue(any(r[\"id\"] == req_id for r in resp.json()))\n\n    def test_invoice_flow_and_commission(self):\n        # Register and login\n        self.register_user(\"alice\", \"password123\", \"customer\")\n        self.register_user(\"bob\", \"password123\", \"provider\")\n        alice_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"alice\", \"password123\")\n        bob_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"bob\", \"password123\")\n        # Create and complete request\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/requests/\", headers=alice_headers, data={\"description\": \"Paint wall\"})\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=bob_headers)\n        self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            headers=bob_headers,\n            data={\"status\": \"in_progress\"}\n        )\n        self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            headers=alice_headers,\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"}\n        )\n        # Check invoices for customer\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers=alice_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = resp.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(invoices), 1)\n        invoice = invoices[0]\n        self.assertEqual(invoice[\"amount\"], 100.0)\n        self.assertEqual(invoice[\"commission\"], 5.0)\n        self.assertFalse(invoice[\"paid\"])\n        invoice_id = invoice[\"id\"]\n        # Pay invoice\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/invoices/{invoice_id}/pay\", headers=alice_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.json()[\"msg\"], \"Invoice marked as paid\")\n        # Confirm paid\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers=alice_headers)\n        self.assertTrue(resp.json()[0][\"paid\"])\n        # Provider sees invoice\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers=bob_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(len(resp.json()), 1)\n        # Customer cannot pay someone else's invoice\n        self.register_user(\"eve\", \"password123\", \"customer\")\n        eve_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"eve\", \"password123\")\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/invoices/{invoice_id}/pay\", headers=eve_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n\n    def test_admin_panel_access_and_management(self):\n        # Register admin, customer, provider\n        self.register_user(\"admin\", \"adminpass\", \"admin\")\n        self.register_user(\"alice\", \"password123\", \"customer\")\n        self.register_user(\"bob\", \"password123\", \"provider\")\n        admin_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"admin\", \"adminpass\")\n        alice_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"alice\", \"password123\")\n        # Non-admin cannot access admin endpoints\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/admin/users\", headers=alice_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        # Admin can list users\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/admin/users\", headers=admin_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        users = resp.json()\n        self.assertTrue(any(u[\"username\"] == \"admin\" for u in users))\n        # Admin can deactivate a user\n        alice_id = next(u[\"id\"] for u in users if u[\"username\"] == \"alice\")\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/admin/users/{alice_id}/deactivate\", headers=admin_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.json()[\"msg\"], \"User deactivated\")\n        # Deactivated user cannot login\n        resp = self.login_user(\"alice\", \"password123\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        token = resp.json()[\"access_token\"]\n        # Try to access as deactivated user\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/requests/me\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.json()[\"detail\"], \"Inactive user\")\n        # Admin can list requests and invoices\n        # Create request and complete for invoice\n        self.register_user(\"carol\", \"password123\", \"customer\")\n        self.register_user(\"dave\", \"password123\", \"provider\")\n        carol_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"carol\", \"password123\")\n        dave_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"dave\", \"password123\")\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/requests/\", headers=carol_headers, data={\"description\": \"Clean house\"})\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=dave_headers)\n        self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            headers=dave_headers,\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"}\n        )\n        # List all requests\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/admin/requests\", headers=admin_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertTrue(any(r[\"description\"] == \"Clean house\" for r in resp.json()))\n        # List all invoices\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/admin/invoices\", headers=admin_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertTrue(any(inv[\"amount\"] == 100.0 for inv in resp.json()))\n\n    def test_edge_case_invalid_status_update(self):\n        # Register customer and provider\n        self.register_user(\"alice\", \"password123\", \"customer\")\n        self.register_user(\"bob\", \"password123\", \"provider\")\n        alice_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"alice\", \"password123\")\n        bob_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"bob\", \"password123\")\n        # Customer creates request\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/requests/\", headers=alice_headers, data={\"description\": \"Test\"})\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        # Try to update status before provider accepts\n        resp = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            headers=alice_headers,\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Try to update with invalid status value\n        resp = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            headers=alice_headers,\n            data={\"status\": \"not_a_status\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 422)  # FastAPI validation error\n\n    def test_provider_cannot_create_request(self):\n        self.register_user(\"bob\", \"password123\", \"provider\")\n        bob_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"bob\", \"password123\")\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/requests/\", headers=bob_headers, data={\"description\": \"Should fail\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.json()[\"detail\"], \"Not a customer\")\n\n    def test_customer_cannot_access_provider_profile(self):\n        self.register_user(\"alice\", \"password123\", \"customer\")\n        alice_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"alice\", \"password123\")\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/providers/me\", headers=alice_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 403)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.json()[\"detail\"], \"Not a provider\")\n\n    def test_invoice_list_empty_for_new_user(self):\n        self.register_user(\"alice\", \"password123\", \"customer\")\n        alice_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"alice\", \"password123\")\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/invoices/me\", headers=alice_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.json(), [])\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    unittest.main()",

Create a request first\n        r = client.post(\"/requests/\", data={\"description\": \"Paint my wall\"},\n                        headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(r.status_code, 200)\n        req_id = r.json()[\"id\"]\n        # List available requests\n        r2 = client.get(\"/requests/available\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(r2.status_code, 200)\n        available = r2.json()\n        ids = [req[\"id\"] for req in available]\n        self.assertIn(req_id, ids)\n        # Create request\n        r = client.post(\"/requests/\", data={\"description\": \"Clean my house\"},\n                        headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"})\n        req_id = r.json()[\"id\"]\n        # Accept request\n        client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"})\n        # Provider updates status to in_progress\n        r2 = client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\", data={\"status\": ServiceStatus.in_progress.value},\n                         headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(r2.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(ServiceStatus.in_progress.value, r2.text)\n        # \"\"\"Update status of a service request (live status updates).\"\"\"\n    req = db.query(ServiceRequest).filter(ServiceRequest.id == request_id).first()\n    if not req:\n        raise current_user.id:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail=\"Not authorized\")\n    if current_user.role == UserRole.customer and req.customer_id != current_user.id:\n        raise commission=commission,\n            paid=False\n        )\n        db.add(invoice)\n        db.commit()\n    return {\"msg\": f\"Status updated to {status}\"}\n\n# --- INVOICING Setup: customer creates request\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/requests/\",\n            data={\"description\": \"Wash my car\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        req_id = response.json()[\"id\"]\n\n        # Customer pays invoice\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/invoices/{inv_id}/pay\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Invoice marked as paid\", response.text)\n\n        # self.register_user(\"bob\", \"pass456\", \"provider\")\n        customer_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"alice\", \"pass123\")\n        provider_headers = self.get_auth_header(\"bob\", \"pass456\")\n        # Customer creates request\n        resp = self.client.post(\"/requests/\", data={\"description\": \"Clean my house\"}, headers=customer_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        req_id = resp.json()[\"id\"]\n        # Provider sees available requests\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/requests/available\", headers=provider_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        available = resp.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(available), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(available[0][\"id\"], req_id)\n        # Provider accepts request\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\", headers=provider_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Provider's requests\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/requests/me\", headers=provider_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        reqs = resp.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(reqs), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(reqs[0][\"id\"], req_id)\n        # Customer's requests\n        resp = self.client.get(\"/requests/me\", headers=customer_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        reqs = resp.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(reqs), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(reqs[0][\"id\"], req_id)\n        # Provider updates status to in_progress\n        resp = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"in_progress\"},\n            headers=provider_headers\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Provider updates status to completed (should create invoice)\n        resp = self.client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"},\n            headers=provider_headers\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Customer views invoice\n        resp = pays invoice\n        inv_id = invoice[\"id\"]\n        resp = self.client.post(f\"/invoices/{inv_id}/pay\", headers=customer_headers)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        #
