--- PROVIDER PROFILE TESTS ---\n\n    def test_list_providers(self):\n        response = client.get(\"/providers/\")\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        providers = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(providers), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(providers[0][\"username\"], self.provider_username)\n\n    def test_get_and_update_provider_profile(self):\n        # Get profile\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/providers/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(response.json()[\"full_name\"], \"\")\n\n        # Update profile\n        response = client.put(\n            \"/providers/me\",\n            data={\n                \"full_name\": \"John Doe\",\n                \"bio\": \"Experienced handyman\",\n                \"skills\": \"plumbing, electrical\"\n            },\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n\n        # Get profile again\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/providers/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        data = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"full_name\"], \"John Doe\")\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"bio\"], \"Experienced handyman\")\n        self.assertEqual(data[\"skills\"], \"plumbing, electrical\")\n\n    def test_provider_profile_access_forbidden(self):\n        # Customer cannot access provider profile endpoints\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/providers/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 403)\n        self.assertIn(\"Not a provider\", response.text)\n\n    # --- SERVICE REQUESTS TESTS ---\n\n    def test_create_and_list_service_request(self):\n        # Customer creates request\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/requests/\",\n            data={\"description\": \"Fix my sink\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        req_id = response.json()[\"id\"]\n\n        # Customer lists own requests\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/requests/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        requests = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(requests), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(requests[0][\"id\"], req_id)\n        self.assertEqual(requests[0][\"status\"], \"requested\")\n\n        # Provider sees available requests\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/requests/available\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        avail = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(avail), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(avail[0][\"id\"], req_id)\n\n    def test_provider_accept_and_update_status(self):\n        # Setup: customer creates request\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/requests/\",\n            data={\"description\": \"Paint my fence\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        req_id = response.json()[\"id\"]\n\n        # Provider accepts request\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Request accepted\", response.text)\n\n        # Provider updates status to in_progress\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"in_progress\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Status updated to in_progress\", response.text)\n\n        # Provider updates status to completed (should trigger invoice)\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Status updated to completed\", response.text)\n\n        # Provider sees invoice\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/invoices/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(invoices), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(invoices[0][\"amount\"], 100.0)\n        self.assertEqual(invoices[0][\"commission\"], 5.0)\n        self.assertFalse(invoices[0][\"paid\"])\n\n    def test_update_status_unauthorized(self):\n        # Setup: customer creates request\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/requests/\",\n            data={\"description\": \"Wash my car\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        req_id = response.json()[\"id\"]\n\n        # Provider tries to update status before accepting (should fail)\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"in_progress\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 403)\n\n        # Customer tries to update status to completed before provider assigned (should work)\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n\n    # --- INVOICING TESTS ---\n\n    def test_invoice_payment(self):\n        # Setup: customer creates and provider completes request\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/requests/\",\n            data={\"description\": \"Clean my house\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        req_id = response.json()[\"id\"]\n        client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n\n        # Customer sees invoice\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/invoices/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        invoices = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(invoices), 1)\n        inv_id = invoices[0][\"id\"]\n        self.assertFalse(invoices[0][\"paid\"])\n\n        # Customer pays invoice\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/invoices/{inv_id}/pay\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Invoice marked as paid\", response.text)\n\n        # Invoice is now paid\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/invoices/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertTrue(response.json()[0][\"paid\"])\n\n    def test_invoice_payment_unauthorized(self):\n        # Setup: customer creates and provider completes request\n        response = client.post(\n            \"/requests/\",\n            data={\"description\": \"Mow my lawn\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.customer_token}\"}\n        )\n        req_id = response.json()[\"id\"]\n        client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/accept\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        client.post(\n            f\"/requests/{req_id}/status\",\n            data={\"status\": \"completed\"},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n\n        # Provider tries to pay invoice (should fail)\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/invoices/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        inv_id = response.json()[0][\"id\"]\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/invoices/{inv_id}/pay\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 403)\n\n    # --- ADMIN PANEL TESTS ---\n\n    def test_admin_list_users_and_deactivate(self):\n        # List all users\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/admin/users\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        users = response.json()\n        self.assertEqual(len(users), 3)  # 1 customer, 1 provider, 1 admin\n\n        # Deactivate provider\n        provider_id = [u for u in users if u[\"username\"] == self.provider_username][0][\"id\"]\n        response = client.post(\n            f\"/admin/users/{provider_id}/deactivate\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.admin_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"User deactivated\", response.text)\n\n        # Provider cannot login anymore (simulate by disabling token use)\n        # Actually, token is still valid, but the system checks is_active\n        # Try to access provider endpoint\n        response = client.get(\n            \"/providers/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {self.provider_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"Inactive user\", response.text)\n\n    def test_admin_list_requests_and_invoices(self):\n        #
